In the grand scheme of things, this is obviously a 1st world problem, but in regards to making the decision to keep the rectangular system, Iâve noticed that even you havenât made your mind up. I believe a rectangle display works as a fantastic method for displaying IG Reels, but I think we can all agree that squares are a foundational display method. I would suggest maybe adding an option in the settings menu so users, like myself, have the option to display a rectangular or square profile feed at their own discretion.
